This is my Yelp review for Dr Back in 2012. It still holds true today.

My children and I have been going to Dr Baick for over 12 (19 as of March 2019) years now and I recommend him to everyone who is looking for a doctor.  About 7 years ago when I went to see him he asked who was my regular doctor, I told him "If any other doctor asked me that question I would tell them that it was you!" His response after looking at my charts was that he had not seen me for over 4 years (in my defense I hadn't been sick) and if he was to be my doctor he would expect to see me at least annually.  With that I have seen him more than annually ever since and he has worked with me to get my health better than it has been my entire adult life.

He is a doctor that takes more time with you then he should.  He spends this time making sure you understand how you are doing in non medical jargon and to learn more about who your are as well as the how you are. He knows about my activities, my children, their health, he even talks with me about my rescue dog and his experience with training them (dogs).  He gets to know his patients at a personal level and I believe it makes him a better doctor because he can tell when you are healthy and when you are not.  I have had him notice when I took one of my children to the walk in (a few doors down from his office) and pull them in to take care of them because they are his patients.

His office staff is friendly and professional.  They have started using an online system, PatientFusion, which allows me to see my labs, past appointments, prognosis, and more.   I like that I can access this information on line.

I know that he is part of the Anthem Blue Cross Prudent Buyer Network and I have never been balanced billed for the write off amounts (of course you have to pay for Copay's and Deductibles) as I have been by other doctors.<//Text>

< Review>
They do serve both hookah and alcohol, but our waitress did not know what Pinot Noir is LOL, they only have 2 types of wine: red and white, where red is $8 a glass and white is $35 a glass. A small bottle of water is $7. Unbelievable nayebalovo.
Hookah lasts only 20 minutes of non-stop smoking (or smoking for 2-3 people) and costs 40 bucks. They do replace coals, but it doesn't do anything for burnt out tobacco. Food is subpar.
The place itself looks nice and there are a couple areas to take pictures, hence the 1 star.
I am planning another night out with friends and thought to come here, but just looked at the photo of our last receipt and realized that this place is not worth coming back.
Although it's nice to not have to wear a mask.< /Review>

<Name>Karen Kovach< /Name><Time>1610576005653</Time><rating>2</rating>< text>
We went to Russell Cellular because they were the only retailer we could find who had the iPhone 12 red with 256GB.  Marilyn G. sold us the phones and migrated the data from our old phones to the new ones which was a great service that we found out later cost $25 each phone. This was a good service, however, we should have been told it would cost $25.  In all the years we have owned cell phones, we were never charged for this migration. We were also told that we could pay for everything but the final $100 per phone that would be on an installment plan or we could pay it off in the next month. Never had this type of charge before either.  Our bill showed the $960 cost per phone and the $100 Installment Amount per phone. In the Your Total column the $100 showed a credit--I will have to pursue this because I just paid the $200 to cover both phones.

On my Verizon bill I found a $40 upgrade fee per phone and  we were signed up for the Verizon Protect Plan, neither of which we were told or asked about.  The Verizon Representative said it was the Cellular Company that added these charges, but Marilyn G. just told me at Russell Cellular that it was Verizon and that I could call and have it reversed.  I had already spent a lot of time with the Verizon Representative and she was not able to reverse the charge.  Marilyn G. removed the monthly Verizon Protect Plan from both of our phones and supposedly reversed the first charges that were made on our Verizon Bill. I expressed my unhappiness with these additional charges that were added without our knowledge and told Marilyn G. that she needs to tell/ask her customers for any additional charges added to the cost of new phones.

My advise if you enter Russell Cellular is to ask for any additional charges to be explained before they are added to your bill.  And I would still like to understand why we couldn't pay off both phones but instead had to finance $200 of the cost. Shady dealings in my book!

**Followup--Jan. 13, 2021--I sent in a complaint on the web to the Better Business Bureau and on Yelp on Jan. 12 and received a call from Verizon Headquarters on Jan 13.  The Verizon Rep. reversed all of the charges that we did not authorize and gave me the new amount of my next Verizon bill.  They responded immediately after they got the complaint from the BBB which was very impressive!  The Rep indicated that they would be contacting Russell Cellular for "counseling."  And interestingly, I was going to add the above information to my Yelp complaint, but can't find Russell Cellular on the Yelp website anywhere.< /text>

<user_id>110256828667258649430< /user_id><username>Andrew Handleman</username>< Date>
1629310971663<//Date>
< rating>
5< /rating>
< Text>
Byram has been businesslike and good to me. In the medical field, they need to coordinate both with your doctor and your medical insurance. Problems arise because so many people are involved, including front desk and medical subordinates. This requires the patient (me) to be involved and, when necessary, prod others to make ends meet. Original post written November 2018

An awesome place to call home!

We've been here about 2 months, and so far I have found nothing negative about this place. The views of Petco Park, Point Loma and the Pacific Ocean from our higher floor are absolutely stunning.

The appliances are brand new and top-notch, and the geek in me just loves the fact that I was able to choose which fiber internet provider I wanted - AT&T or Cox. Both offer full gig speeds up and down here at the building. Throw in the eight CAT6 network drops that are located throughout the apartment and you have a home network that is pretty much the envy of any tech person - which is who they are probably targeting.

The central A/C works great. The floor to ceiling windows in the living room and bedroom are very nice. There‚Äôs nothing quite like waking up and looking at Petco Park or watching a Navy ship return to port.

Parking is provided via the gated underground garage.  First space is free, unlike other downtown apartments that charge over $100 per month for your first parking spot. Parking spaces are wide, which is probably a good thing, as there are a lot of high end cars in the garage.  The proximity of the Gaslamp Quarter is just icing on the cake.

I almost forgot to mention the staff.  They are wonderful.

What's not to love :)

UPDATE - 11 May

I still give this place 5 stars. All of the amenities are now up and running. No issues with the homeless like some other reviewers have stated. Area around Park 12 is MUCH better than the rest of East Village - It‚Äôs all part of living downtown.

I will definitely renew my lease :)</text>

<pictures>None< /pictures><review>Raised my rent on a 10x10 unit $100 in one shot with barely any notice. I'd be better off setting all my belongings on fire and buying new stuff when needed. I'm working on recycling, donating and selling everything and will be moving out as soon as I can.

EDIT: To respond to Extra Space's reply- I already did call and the local office said that "corporate" sets the rates and that they'll have "someone" call me to "talk" about it. I asked who that would be so that I could make the call to the right people and the answer was an ambiguous "someone" up the chain.

I won't change my review. This was a bait and switch. And, it turns out that Extra Space has had a class action lawsuit filed recently (Johnson et al. v. Extra Space Storage Inc.) alleging that ExtraSpace is using bait-and-switch to lure people in at lower rates and then jacking up the rent astronomically once they've spent weeks painstakingly moving everything into their storage units.

TL;DR ExtraSpace will jack up your rent 10%-50% about every 6 months. My most recent increase was 50% after not even 6 months. They are currently being sued for bait-and-switch. Do a google search for "Class Action Lawsuit Extra Space" to see what you'll be getting in to.< /review><user>105789266030026787662< /user>< Response>

<userid>116413415978657913876</userid><username>John B< /username><time>1457141085349</time>< review>
Be prepared for significant price increases just a few months after renting here.  Month-to-month seems like a renter-friendly policy until they raise prices (and we're not talking small increases) at the worst possible time (they know you're kind of locked-in if you have a large unit, even though it's a monthly contract).  I'm accustomed to small price increases after a year, but what they do is almost unethical (although not technically illegal).  They need to be more upfront about this, especially for an Alameda-based business.

Note: I used Extra Space in another city for almost three years, and I never once had this issue, so I'm not sure if I believe the "Decisions are made by corporate headquarters, it's out of our control" line.

They could also give their facilities a facelift, and not just their front entrance and main office (which are freshly painted for their website photos).  Hallways are damp (smell like mold), dark, and narrow, and the lightweight partitions seem like they can easily be broken into.  Not good considering their location is next to a lot of vacant warehouses and old industrial buildings on a poorly lit street.  Since I'm not storing anything of value, I can deal with dated facilities.  But I never feel comfortable going here alone at dark.</review>
